### IBM COS (S3)

Information 已存储 与 IBM Cloud 对象 存储 是 已加密 和 dispersed across
多个 geographic locations, 和 accessed 通过 一个 implementation 的 该 S3 API.
这 service makes 使用 的 该 distributed 存储 technologies provided 由 IBM’s
Cloud 对象 存储 System (formerly Cleversafe). 用于 更多 information visit:
<http://www.ibm.com/cloud/object-storage>

到 配置 访问 到 IBM COS S3, follow 该 steps below:

1. Run rclone 配置 和 select n 用于 一个 新 remote.

   ```text
   2018/02/14 14:13:11 NOTICE: Config file "C:\\Users\\a\\.config\\rclone\\rclone.conf" not found - using defaults
   No remotes found, make a new one?
   n) New remote
   s) Set configuration password
   q) Quit config
   n/s/q> n
   ```

2. Enter 该 name 用于 该 configuration

   ```text
   name> <YOUR NAME>
   ```

3. Select "s3" storage.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   [snip]
   XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
      \ "s3"
   [snip]
   Storage> s3
   ```

4. Select IBM COS 作为 该 S3 存储 Provider.

   ```text
   Choose the S3 provider.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
      1 / Choose this option to configure Storage to AWS S3
        \ "AWS"
      2 / Choose this option to configure Storage to Ceph Systems
        \ "Ceph"
      3 /  Choose this option to configure Storage to Dreamhost
        \ "Dreamhost"
      4 / Choose this option to the configure Storage to IBM COS S3
        \ "IBMCOS"
      5 / Choose this option to the configure Storage to Minio
        \ "Minio"
      Provider>4
   ```

5. Enter 该 访问 密钥 和 Secret.

   ```text
   AWS Access Key ID - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   access_key_id> <>
   AWS Secret Access Key (password) - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   secret_access_key> <>
   ```

6. 指定 该 端点 用于 IBM COS. 用于 公共 IBM COS, choose 从 该 option
below. 用于 On Premise IBM COS, enter 一个 端点 address.

   ```text
   Endpoint for IBM COS S3 API.
   Specify if using an IBM COS On Premise.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / US Cross Region Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.us-geo.objectstorage.softlayer.net"
    2 / US Cross Region Dallas Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.dal.us-geo.objectstorage.softlayer.net"
    3 / US Cross Region Washington DC Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.wdc-us-geo.objectstorage.softlayer.net"
    4 / US Cross Region San Jose Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.sjc-us-geo.objectstorage.softlayer.net"
    5 / US Cross Region Private Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.us-geo.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
    6 / US Cross Region Dallas Private Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.dal-us-geo.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
    7 / US Cross Region Washington DC Private Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.wdc-us-geo.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
    8 / US Cross Region San Jose Private Endpoint
      \ "s3-api.sjc-us-geo.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
    9 / US Region East Endpoint
      \ "s3.us-east.objectstorage.softlayer.net"
   10 / US Region East Private Endpoint
      \ "s3.us-east.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
   11 / US Region South Endpoint
   [snip]
   34 / Toronto Single Site Private Endpoint
      \ "s3.tor01.objectstorage.service.networklayer.com"
   endpoint>1
   ```

7. 指定 一个 IBM COS Location Constraint. 该 location constraint 必须 match
端点 当 使用 IBM Cloud Public. 用于 on-prem COS, 做 不 make 一个 selection
从 此 list, hit enter

   ```text
    1 / US Cross Region Standard
      \ "us-standard"
    2 / US Cross Region Vault
      \ "us-vault"
    3 / US Cross Region Cold
      \ "us-cold"
    4 / US Cross Region Flex
      \ "us-flex"
    5 / US East Region Standard
      \ "us-east-standard"
    6 / US East Region Vault
      \ "us-east-vault"
    7 / US East Region Cold
      \ "us-east-cold"
    8 / US East Region Flex
      \ "us-east-flex"
    9 / US South Region Standard
      \ "us-south-standard"
   10 / US South Region Vault
      \ "us-south-vault"
   [snip]
   32 / Toronto Flex
      \ "tor01-flex"
   location_constraint>1
   ```

8. 指定 一个 canned ACL. IBM Cloud (Storage) 支持 "public-read" 和 "private".
IBM Cloud(Infra) 支持 所有 该 canned ACLs. On-Premise COS 支持 所有 the
canned ACLs.

   ```text
   Canned ACL used when creating buckets and/or storing objects in S3.
   For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
         1 / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. No one else has access rights (default). This acl is available on IBM Cloud (Infra), IBM Cloud (Storage), On-Premise COS
         \ "private"
         2  / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. The AllUsers group gets READ access. This acl is available on IBM Cloud (Infra), IBM Cloud (Storage), On-Premise IBM COS
         \ "public-read"
         3 / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. The AllUsers group gets READ and WRITE access. This acl is available on IBM Cloud (Infra), On-Premise IBM COS
         \ "public-read-write"
         4  / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. The AuthenticatedUsers group gets READ access. Not supported on Buckets. This acl is available on IBM Cloud (Infra) and On-Premise IBM COS
         \ "authenticated-read"
   acl> 1
   ```

9. Review 该 已显示 配置 和 accept 到 保存 该 "remote" 然后 quit.
该 配置 文件 应该 look like this

   ```ini
   [xxx]
   type = s3
   Provider = IBMCOS
   access_key_id = xxx
   secret_access_key = yyy
   endpoint = s3-api.us-geo.objectstorage.softlayer.net
   location_constraint = us-standard
   acl = private
   ```

10. Execute rclone commands

   ```text
   1) Create a bucket.
      rclone mkdir IBM-COS-XREGION:newbucket
   2) List available buckets.
      rclone lsd IBM-COS-XREGION:
      -1 2017-11-08 21:16:22        -1 test
      -1 2018-02-14 20:16:39        -1 newbucket
   3) List contents of a bucket.
       rclone ls IBM-COS-XREGION:newbucket
       18685952 test.exe
   4) Copy a file from local to remote.
      rclone copy /Users/file.txt IBM-COS-XREGION:newbucket
   5) Copy a file from remote to local.
      rclone copy IBM-COS-XREGION:newbucket/file.txt .
   6) Delete a file on remote.
      rclone delete IBM-COS-XREGION:newbucket/file.txt
   ```

#### IBM IAM authentication

如果 使用 IBM IAM authentication 与 IBM API KEY 您 need 到 fill 在 these
additional parameters

1. Select false 用于 env_auth
2. Leave `access_key_id` 和 `secret_access_key` blank
3. Paste 您的 `ibm_api_key`

   ```text
   Option ibm_api_key.
   IBM API Key to be used to obtain IAM token
   Enter a value of type string. Press Enter for the default (1).
   ibm_api_key>
   ```

4. Paste 您的 `ibm_resource_instance_id`

   ```text
   Option ibm_resource_instance_id.
   IBM service instance id
   Enter a value of type string. Press Enter for the default (2).
   ibm_resource_instance_id>
   ```

5. 在 advanced settings 类型 true 用于 `v2_auth`

   ```text
   Option v2_auth.
   If true use v2 authentication.
   If this is false (the default) then rclone will use v4 authentication.
   If it is set then rclone will use v2 authentication.
   Use this only if v4 signatures don't work, e.g. pre Jewel/v10 CEPH.
   Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default (true).
   v2_auth>
   ```

这里 是 一个 示例 的 making 一个 [IDrive e2](https://www.idrive.com/e2/)

```console

```

```text

   \ (s3)

Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
XX / IDrive e2
   \ (IDrive)
[snip]

Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>

Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> YOUR_ACCESS_KEY

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> YOUR_SECRET_KEY

Option acl.
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (public-read)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 3 | The AllUsers group gets READ and WRITE access.
   | Granting this on a bucket is generally not recommended.
   \ (public-read-write)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 4 | The AuthenticatedUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (authenticated-read)
   / Object owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 5 | Bucket owner gets READ access.
   | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-read)
   / Both the object owner and the bucket owner get FULL_CONTROL over the object.
 6 | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-full-control)
acl>

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n>

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: IDrive
- access_key_id: YOUR_ACCESS_KEY
- secret_access_key: YOUR_SECRET_KEY
- endpoint: q9d9.la12.idrivee2-5.com
Keep this "e2" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

### IONOS Cloud {#ionos}

[IONOS S3 对象存储](https://cloud.ionos.com/storage/object-storage) 是
service offered 由 IONOS 用于 存储 和 accessing unstructured data.
到 连接 到 该 service, 您 将 need 一个 访问 密钥 和 一个 秘密 key. These
可以 是 found 在 该 [Data Center Designer](https://dcd.ionos.com/), by
selecting **Manager resources** > **对象 存储 密钥 Manager**.

这里 是 一个 示例 的 一个 configuration. First, run `rclone config`. 这 will
walk 您 通过 一个 interactive setup process. 类型 `n` 到 add 该 新 remote,
和 然后 enter 一个 name:

```text
Enter name for new remote.
name> ionos-fra
```

类型 `s3` 到 choose 该 连接 type:

```text
Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
[snip]
XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
   \ (s3)
[snip]
Storage> s3
```

类型 `IONOS`:

```text
Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
XX / IONOS Cloud
   \ (IONOS)
[snip]
provider> IONOS
```

Press Enter 到 choose 该 默认 选项 `Enter AWS 凭据 在 该 下一个 step`:

```text
Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>
```

Enter 您的 访问 密钥 和 秘密 key. 这些 可以 是 已检索 在 the
[Data Center Designer](https://dcd.ionos.com/), click on 该 menu
"Manager resources" / "对象 存储 密钥 Manager".

```text
Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> YOUR_ACCESS_KEY

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> YOUR_SECRET_KEY
```

Choose 该 区域 哪里 您的 桶 是 located:

```text
Option region.
Region where your bucket will be created and your data stored.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / Frankfurt, Germany
   \ (de)
 2 / Berlin, Germany
   \ (eu-central-2)
 3 / Logrono, Spain
   \ (eu-south-2)
region> 2
```

Choose 该 端点 从 该 same region:

```text
Option endpoint.
Endpoint for IONOS S3 Object Storage.
Specify the endpoint from the same region.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / Frankfurt, Germany
   \ (s3-eu-central-1.ionoscloud.com)
 2 / Berlin, Germany
   \ (s3-eu-central-2.ionoscloud.com)
 3 / Logrono, Spain
   \ (s3-eu-south-2.ionoscloud.com)
endpoint> 1
```

Press Enter 到 choose 该 默认 选项 或 choose 该 desired ACL setting:

```text
Option acl.
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
[snip]
acl>
```

Press Enter 到 skip 该 advanced config:

```text
Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n>
```

Press Enter 到 保存 该 configuration, 和 然后 `q` 到 quit 该 配置 process:

```text
Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: IONOS
- access_key_id: YOUR_ACCESS_KEY
- secret_access_key: YOUR_SECRET_KEY
- endpoint: s3-eu-central-1.ionoscloud.com
Keep this "ionos-fra" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

Done! 现在 您 可以 try 一些 commands (用于 macOS, 使用 `./rclone` 代替 的 `rclone`).

1) 创建 一个 桶 (该 name 必须 是 unique 在...内 该 整个 IONOS S3)

   ```console
   rclone mkdir ionos-fra:my-bucket
   ```

2) List 可用 buckets

   ```console
   rclone lsd ionos-fra:
   ```

3) 复制 一个 文件 从 本地 到 remote

   ```console
   rclone copy /Users/file.txt ionos-fra:my-bucket
   ```

4) List contents 的 一个 bucket

   ```console
   rclone ls ionos-fra:my-bucket
   ```

5) 复制 一个 文件 从 远程 到 local

   ```console
   rclone copy ionos-fra:my-bucket/file.txt
   ```

### Leviia Cloud 对象 存储 {#leviia}

[Leviia 对象存储](https://www.leviia.com/object-storage/)，备份和安全
您的 data 在 一个 100% French cloud, independent 的 GAFAM..

到 配置 访问 到 Leviia, follow 该 steps below:

1. Run `rclone config` 和 select `n` 用于 一个 新 remote.

   ```text
   rclone config
   No remotes found, make a new one?
   n) New remote
   s) Set configuration password
   q) Quit config
   n/s/q> n
   ```

2. Give 该 name 的 该 configuration. 用于 example, name it 'leviia'.

   ```text
   name> leviia
   ```

3. Select `s3` storage.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   [snip]
   XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
      \ (s3)
   [snip]
   Storage> s3
   ```

4. Select `Leviia` provider.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   1 / Amazon Web Services (AWS) S3
      \ "AWS"
   [snip]
   15 / Leviia Object Storage
      \ (Leviia)
   [snip]
   provider> Leviia
   ```

5. Enter 您的 SecretId 和 SecretKey 的 Leviia.

   ```text
   Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
   Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
   Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default ("false").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
      \ "false"
    2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
      \ "true"
   env_auth> 1
   AWS Access Key ID.
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   access_key_id> ZnIx.xxxxxxxxxxxxxxx
   AWS Secret Access Key (password)
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   secret_access_key> xxxxxxxxxxx
   ```

6. Select 端点 用于 Leviia.

   ```text
      / The default endpoint
    1 | Leviia.
      \ (s3.leviia.com)
   [snip]
   endpoint> 1
   ```

7. Choose acl.

   ```text
   Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
   doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
      / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
    1 | No one else has access rights (default).
      \ (private)
      / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
    2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
      \ (public-read)
   [snip]
   acl> 1
   Edit advanced config? (y/n)
   y) Yes
   n) No (default)
   y/n> n
   Remote config
   --------------------
   [leviia]
   - type: s3
   - provider: Leviia
   - access_key_id: ZnIx.xxxxxxx
   - secret_access_key: xxxxxxxx
   - endpoint: s3.leviia.com
   - acl: private
   --------------------
   y) Yes this is OK (default)
   e) Edit this remote
   d) Delete this remote
   y/e/d> y
   Current remotes:

   Name                 Type
   ====                 ====
   leviia                s3
   ```


```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
n/s> n
name> Liara
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
[snip]
XX / Amazon S3 (also Dreamhost, Ceph, ChinaMobile, ArvanCloud, Liara, Minio)
   \ "s3"
[snip]
Storage> s3
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars). Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
   \ "false"
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
   \ "true"
env_auth> 1
AWS Access Key ID - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
access_key_id> YOURACCESSKEY
AWS Secret Access Key (password) - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
secret_access_key> YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
Region to connect to.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   / The default endpoint
 1 | US Region, Northern Virginia, or Pacific Northwest.
   | Leave location constraint empty.
   \ "us-east-1"
[snip]
region>
Endpoint for S3 API.
Leave blank if using Liara to use the default endpoint for the region.
Specify if using an S3 clone such as Ceph.
endpoint> storage.iran.liara.space
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and/or storing objects in S3.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. No one else has access rights (default).
   \ "private"
[snip]
acl>
The server-side encryption algorithm used when storing this object in S3.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / None
   \ ""
 2 / AES256
   \ "AES256"
server_side_encryption>
The storage class to use when storing objects in S3.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Default
   \ ""
 2 / Standard storage class
   \ "STANDARD"
storage_class>
Remote config
--------------------
[Liara]
env_auth = false
access_key_id = YOURACCESSKEY
secret_access_key = YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
endpoint = storage.iran.liara.space
location_constraint =
acl =
server_side_encryption =
storage_class =
--------------------
y) Yes this is OK
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

```ini
[Liara]
type = s3
provider = Liara
env_auth = false
access_key_id = YOURACCESSKEY
secret_access_key = YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
region =
endpoint = storage.iran.liara.space
location_constraint =
acl =
server_side_encryption =
storage_class =
```

```text
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
the default (private) will be used.
```

### Minio

[Minio](https://minio.io/) 是 一个 对象 存储 服务器 built 用于 cloud application
developers 和 devops.

It 是 very easy 到 install 和 provides 一个 S3 compatible 服务器 哪个 可以 是 used
由 rclone.

要使用它，请按照 [这里](https://docs.minio.io/docs/minio-quickstart-guide) 的说明安装 Minio。

当 it 配置 itself Minio 将 print something like this

```text
Endpoint:  http://192.168.1.106:9000  http://172.23.0.1:9000
AccessKey: USWUXHGYZQYFYFFIT3RE
SecretKey: MOJRH0mkL1IPauahWITSVvyDrQbEEIwljvmxdq03
Region:    us-east-1
SQS ARNs:  arn:minio:sqs:us-east-1:1:redis arn:minio:sqs:us-east-1:2:redis

Browser Access:
   http://192.168.1.106:9000  http://172.23.0.1:9000

Command-line Access: https://docs.minio.io/docs/minio-client-quickstart-guide
   $ mc config host add myminio http://192.168.1.106:9000 USWUXHGYZQYFYFFIT3RE MOJRH0mkL1IPauahWITSVvyDrQbEEIwljvmxdq03

Object API (Amazon S3 compatible):
   Go:         https://docs.minio.io/docs/golang-client-quickstart-guide
   Java:       https://docs.minio.io/docs/java-client-quickstart-guide
   Python:     https://docs.minio.io/docs/python-client-quickstart-guide
   JavaScript: https://docs.minio.io/docs/javascript-client-quickstart-guide
   .NET:       https://docs.minio.io/docs/dotnet-client-quickstart-guide

Drive Capacity: 26 GiB Free, 165 GiB Total
```

这些 details need 到 go 到 `rclone config` like this.  Note 该 it
是 important 到 put 该 区域 在 作为 stated above.

```text
env_auth> 1
access_key_id> USWUXHGYZQYFYFFIT3RE
secret_access_key> MOJRH0mkL1IPauahWITSVvyDrQbEEIwljvmxdq03
region> us-east-1
endpoint> http://192.168.1.106:9000
location_constraint>
server_side_encryption>
```

哪个 makes 该 配置 文件 look like this

```ini
[minio]
type = s3
provider = Minio
env_auth = false
access_key_id = USWUXHGYZQYFYFFIT3RE
secret_access_key = MOJRH0mkL1IPauahWITSVvyDrQbEEIwljvmxdq03
region = us-east-1
endpoint = http://192.168.1.106:9000
location_constraint =
server_side_encryption =
```

所以 一旦 设置 up, 用于 example, 到 复制 files 到 一个 bucket

```console
rclone copy /path/to/files minio:bucket
```

### Netease NOS

用于 Netease NOS 配置 作为 per 该 configurator `rclone config`
设置 该 提供者 `Netease`.  这 将 automatically set
`force_path_style = false` 哪个 是 必要 用于 it 到 run properly.

### Outscale

[OUTSCALE 对象 存储 (OOS)](https://en.outscale.com/storage/outscale-object-storage/)
是 一个 enterprise-grade, S3-compatible 存储 service provided 由 OUTSCALE,
一个 brand 的 Dassault Systèmes. 用于 更多 information 关于 OOS, 参阅 the
[官方文档](https://docs.outscale.com/en/userguide/OUTSCALE-Object-Storage-OOS.html)。

这里 是 一个 示例 的 一个 OOS 配置 该 您 可以 paste 到 您的 rclone
配置 file:

```ini
[outscale]
type = s3
provider = Outscale
env_auth = false
access_key_id = ABCDEFGHIJ0123456789
secret_access_key = XXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXXX
region = eu-west-2
endpoint = oos.eu-west-2.outscale.com
acl = private
```

您 可以 也 run `rclone config` 到 go 通过 该 interactive setup process:

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n
```

```text
Enter name for new remote.
name> outscale
```

```text
[snip]

   \ (s3)
[snip]

```

```text

Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
the default (private) will be used.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
[snip]
```

### OVHcloud {#ovhcloud}

[OVHcloud 对象存储](https://www.ovhcloud.com/en-ie/public-cloud/object-storage/)
是 一个 S3-compatible general-purpose 对象 存储 platform 可用 在 all
OVHcloud regions. 到 使用 该 platform, 您 将 need 一个 访问 密钥 和 秘密 key.
到 know 更多 关于 it 和 how 到 interact 与 该 platform, take 一个 look 在 the
[documentation](https://ovh.to/8stqhuo).

这里 是 一个 示例 的 making 一个 OVHcloud 对象 存储 配置 with
`rclone config`:

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> ovhcloud-rbx

Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
[...]
 XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, Alibaba, ArvanCloud, Ceph, ChinaMobile, Cloudflare, DigitalOcean, Dreamhost, GCS, HuaweiOBS, IBMCOS, IDrive, IONOS, LyveCloud, Leviia, Liara, Linode, Magalu, Minio, Netease, Outscale, OVHcloud, Petabox, RackCorp, Rclone, Scaleway, SeaweedFS, Selectel, Storj, Synology, TencentCOS, Wasabi, Qiniu and others
   \ (s3)
[...]

Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[...]
XX / OVHcloud Object Storage
   \ (OVHcloud)
[...]

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth> 1

Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> my_access

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> my_secret

Option region.
Region where your bucket will be created and your data stored.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / Gravelines, France
   \ (gra)
 2 / Roubaix, France
   \ (rbx)
 3 / Strasbourg, France
   \ (sbg)
 4 / Paris, France (3AZ)
   \ (eu-west-par)

   \ (de)

   \ (uk)

   \ (waw)

   \ (bhs)

   \ (ca-east-tor)

   \ (sgp)

   \ (ap-southeast-syd)

   \ (ap-south-mum)

   \ (us-east-va)

   \ (us-west-or)
15 / Roubaix, France (Cold Archive)
   \ (rbx-archive)
region> 2

Option endpoint.
Endpoint for OVHcloud Object Storage.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / OVHcloud Gravelines, France
   \ (s3.gra.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 2 / OVHcloud Roubaix, France
   \ (s3.rbx.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 3 / OVHcloud Strasbourg, France
   \ (s3.sbg.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 4 / OVHcloud Paris, France (3AZ)
   \ (s3.eu-west-par.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 5 / OVHcloud Frankfurt, Germany
   \ (s3.de.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 6 / OVHcloud London, United Kingdom
   \ (s3.uk.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 7 / OVHcloud Warsaw, Poland
   \ (s3.waw.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 8 / OVHcloud Beauharnois, Canada
   \ (s3.bhs.io.cloud.ovh.net)
 9 / OVHcloud Toronto, Canada
   \ (s3.ca-east-tor.io.cloud.ovh.net)
10 / OVHcloud Singapore
   \ (s3.sgp.io.cloud.ovh.net)
11 / OVHcloud Sydney, Australia
   \ (s3.ap-southeast-syd.io.cloud.ovh.net)
12 / OVHcloud Mumbai, India
   \ (s3.ap-south-mum.io.cloud.ovh.net)
13 / OVHcloud Vint Hill, Virginia, USA
   \ (s3.us-east-va.io.cloud.ovh.us)
14 / OVHcloud Hillsboro, Oregon, USA
   \ (s3.us-west-or.io.cloud.ovh.us)
15 / OVHcloud Roubaix, France (Cold Archive)
   \ (s3.rbx-archive.io.cloud.ovh.net)
endpoint> 2

Option acl.
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
the default (private) will be used.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (public-read)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 3 | The AllUsers group gets READ and WRITE access.
   | Granting this on a bucket is generally not recommended.
   \ (public-read-write)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 4 | The AuthenticatedUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (authenticated-read)
   / Object owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 5 | Bucket owner gets READ access.
   | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-read)
   / Both the object owner and the bucket owner get FULL_CONTROL over the object.
 6 | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-full-control)
acl> 1

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n> n

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: OVHcloud
- access_key_id: my_access
- secret_access_key: my_secret
- region: rbx
- endpoint: s3.rbx.io.cloud.ovh.net
- acl: private
Keep this "ovhcloud-rbx" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

您的 配置 文件 应该 现在 look like this:

```ini
[ovhcloud-rbx]
type = s3
provider = OVHcloud
access_key_id = my_access
secret_access_key = my_secret
region = rbx
endpoint = s3.rbx.io.cloud.ovh.net
acl = private
```

### Petabox

这里 是 一个 示例 的 making 一个 [Petabox](https://petabox.io/)
configuration. 第一 run:

```console
rclone config
```

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?

Enter name for new remote.
name> My Petabox Storage

   \ "s3"

 1 / US East (N. Virginia)

For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl

doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
the default (private) will be used.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (public-read)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 3 | The AllUsers group gets READ and WRITE access.
   | Granting this on a bucket is generally not recommended.
   \ (public-read-write)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 4 | The AuthenticatedUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (authenticated-read)
   / Object owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 5 | Bucket owner gets READ access.
   | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-read)
   / Both the object owner and the bucket owner get FULL_CONTROL over the object.
 6 | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-full-control)
acl> 1

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n> No

Configuration complete.

- provider: Petabox
- access_key_id: YOUR_ACCESS_KEY_ID
- secret_access_key: YOUR_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
```

### Pure 存储 FlashBlade

[Pure 存储 FlashBlade](https://www.purestorage.com/products/unstructured-data-storage.html)
是 一个 high performance S3-compatible 对象 store.

FlashBlade 支持 大多数 modern S3 features including:

- ListObjectsV2
- Multipart 上传 与 AWS-compatible ETags
- Advanced 校验和 algorithms (SHA256, CRC32, CRC32C) 与 trailer support
  (Purity//FB 4.4.2+)
- 对象 versioning 和 lifecycle management
- Virtual hosted-style 请求 (要求 DNS configuration)

到 配置 rclone 用于 Pure 存储 FlashBlade:

首先运行：

```console
rclone config
```

这将引导您完成交互式设置过程：

```text
No remotes found, make a new one?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> flashblade

Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
[snip]
 4 / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, Alibaba, ArvanCloud, Ceph, ChinaMobile, Cloudflare, DigitalOcean, Dreamhost, FlashBlade, GCS, HuaweiOBS, IBMCOS, IDrive, IONOS, LyveCloud, Leviia, Liara, Linode, Magalu, Minio, Netease, Outscale, Petabox, RackCorp, Rclone, Scaleway, SeaweedFS, Selectel, Storj, Synology, TencentCOS, Wasabi, Qiniu and others
   \ (s3)
[snip]
Storage> s3

Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
 9 / Pure Storage FlashBlade Object Storage
   \ (FlashBlade)
[snip]
provider> FlashBlade

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth> 1

Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> ACCESS_KEY_ID

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> SECRET_ACCESS_KEY

Option endpoint.
Endpoint for S3 API.
Required when using an S3 clone.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
endpoint> https://s3.flashblade.example.com

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n> n

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: FlashBlade
- access_key_id: ACCESS_KEY_ID
- secret_access_key: SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
- endpoint: https://s3.flashblade.example.com
Keep this "flashblade" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

这 results 在 该 following 配置 是 已存储 在 `~/.config/rclone/rclone.conf`:

```ini
[flashblade]
type = s3
provider = FlashBlade
access_key_id = ACCESS_KEY_ID
secret_access_key = SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
endpoint = https://s3.flashblade.example.com
```

Note: 该 FlashBlade 端点 应该 是 该 S3 data VIP. 用于 virtual-hosted style
requests, ensure proper DNS configuration: subdomains 的 该 端点 hostname should
resolve 到 一个 FlashBlade data VIP. 用于 example, 如果 您的 端点 是 `https://s3.flashblade.example.com`,
然后 `bucket-name.s3.flashblade.example.com` 应该 也 resolve 到 该 data VIP.

### Qiniu Cloud 对象 存储 (Kodo) {#qiniu}

[Qiniu Cloud 对象 存储 (Kodo)](https://www.qiniu.com/en/products/kodo), a
completely independent-researched core technology 哪个 是 proven 由 repeated
客户体验占据绝对领先的市场领导者地位。Kodo
可以 是 widely applied 到 mass data management.

到 配置 访问 到 Qiniu Kodo, follow 该 steps below:

1. Run `rclone config` 和 select `n` 用于 一个 新 remote.

   ```text
   rclone config
   No remotes found, make a new one?
   n) New remote
   s) Set configuration password
   q) Quit config
   n/s/q> n
   ```

2. Give 该 name 的 该 configuration. 用于 example, name it 'qiniu'.

   ```text
   name> qiniu
   ```

3. Select `s3` storage.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   [snip]
   XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
      \ (s3)
   [snip]
   Storage> s3
   ```

4. Select `Qiniu` provider.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   1 / Amazon Web Services (AWS) S3
      \ "AWS"
   [snip]
   22 / Qiniu Object Storage (Kodo)
      \ (Qiniu)
   [snip]
   provider> Qiniu
   ```

5. Enter 您的 SecretId 和 SecretKey 的 Qiniu Kodo.

   ```text
   Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
   Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
   Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default ("false").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
      \ "false"
    2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
      \ "true"
   env_auth> 1
   AWS Access Key ID.
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   access_key_id> AKIDxxxxxxxxxx
   AWS Secret Access Key (password)
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   secret_access_key> xxxxxxxxxxx
   ```

6. Select 端点 用于 Qiniu Kodo. 这 是 该 standard 端点 用于 different region.

   ```text
      / The default endpoint - a good choice if you are unsure.
    1 | East China Region 1.
      | Needs location constraint cn-east-1.
      \ (cn-east-1)
      / East China Region 2.
    2 | Needs location constraint cn-east-2.
      \ (cn-east-2)
      / North China Region 1.
    3 | Needs location constraint cn-north-1.
      \ (cn-north-1)
      / South China Region 1.
    4 | Needs location constraint cn-south-1.
      \ (cn-south-1)
      / North America Region.
    5 | Needs location constraint us-north-1.
      \ (us-north-1)
      / Southeast Asia Region 1.
    6 | Needs location constraint ap-southeast-1.
      \ (ap-southeast-1)
      / Northeast Asia Region 1.
    7 | Needs location constraint ap-northeast-1.
      \ (ap-northeast-1)
   [snip]
   endpoint> 1

   Option endpoint.
   Endpoint for Qiniu Object Storage.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
   Press Enter to leave empty.
    1 / East China Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-cn-east-1.qiniucs.com)
    2 / East China Endpoint 2
      \ (s3-cn-east-2.qiniucs.com)
    3 / North China Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-cn-north-1.qiniucs.com)
    4 / South China Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-cn-south-1.qiniucs.com)
    5 / North America Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-us-north-1.qiniucs.com)
    6 / Southeast Asia Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-ap-southeast-1.qiniucs.com)
    7 / Northeast Asia Endpoint 1
      \ (s3-ap-northeast-1.qiniucs.com)
   endpoint> 1

   Option location_constraint.
   Location constraint - must be set to match the Region.
   Used when creating buckets only.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
   Press Enter to leave empty.
    1 / East China Region 1
      \ (cn-east-1)
    2 / East China Region 2
      \ (cn-east-2)
    3 / North China Region 1
      \ (cn-north-1)
    4 / South China Region 1
      \ (cn-south-1)
    5 / North America Region 1
      \ (us-north-1)
    6 / Southeast Asia Region 1
      \ (ap-southeast-1)
    7 / Northeast Asia Region 1
      \ (ap-northeast-1)
   location_constraint> 1
   ```

7. Choose acl 和 存储 class.

   ```text
   Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
   doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
      / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
    1 | No one else has access rights (default).
      \ (private)
      / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
    2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
      \ (public-read)
   [snip]
   acl> 2
   The storage class to use when storing new objects in Tencent COS.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Standard storage class
      \ (STANDARD)
    2 / Infrequent access storage mode
      \ (LINE)
    3 / Archive storage mode
      \ (GLACIER)
    4 / Deep archive storage mode
      \ (DEEP_ARCHIVE)
   [snip]
   storage_class> 1
   Edit advanced config? (y/n)
   y) Yes
   n) No (default)
   y/n> n
   Remote config
   --------------------
   [qiniu]
   - type: s3
   - provider: Qiniu
   - access_key_id: xxx
   - secret_access_key: xxx
   - region: cn-east-1
   - endpoint: s3-cn-east-1.qiniucs.com
   - location_constraint: cn-east-1
   - acl: public-read
   - storage_class: STANDARD
   --------------------
   y) Yes this is OK (default)
   e) Edit this remote
   d) Delete this remote
   y/e/d> y
   Current remotes:

   Name                 Type
   ====                 ====
   qiniu                s3
   ```

### FileLu S5 {#filelu-s5}

[FileLu S5 对象 Storage](https://s5lu.com) 是 一个 S3-compatible 对象 storage
system. It provides 多个 区域 options (Global, US-East, EU-Central,
AP-Southeast, 和 ME-Central) 当 使用 一个 单个 端点 (`s5lu.com`).
FileLu S5 是 designed 用于 scalability, security, 和 simplicity, 与 predictable
pricing 和 无 hidden charges 用于 data 传输 或 API requests.

这里 是 一个 示例 的 making 一个 configuration.  第一 run:

```console
rclone config
```

这 将 guide 您 通过 一个 interactive setup process.

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?

s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> s5lu

Option Storage.

[snip]

   \ (s3)
[snip]

Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
XX / FileLu S5 Object Storage
   \ (FileLu)
[snip]
provider> FileLu

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>
```

### Rabata {#Rabata}

[Rabata](https://rabata.io) 是 一个 S3-compatible 安全 cloud 存储 service that
offers flat, transparent pricing (无 API 请求 fees) 当 supporting standard
S3 APIs. It 是 suitable 用于 backup, application storage,media workflows, and
archive 使用 cases.

服务器 side 复制 是 不 implemented 与 Rabata, 也 meaning modification time
的 objects 无法 是 updated.

Rclone config:

```text
rclone config
```

### RackCorp {#RackCorp}

[RackCorp 对象 Storage](https://www.rackcorp.com/storage/s3storage) 是 一个 S3
compatible 对象 存储 platform 从 您的 friendly cloud 提供者 RackCorp.
该 service 是 fast, reliable, well priced 和 located 在 许多 strategic
locations unserviced 由 others, 到 ensure 您 可以 maintain data sovereignty.

之前 您 可以 使用 RackCorp 对象 Storage, you'll need to
在我们的 [门户](https://portal.rackcorp.com) 上 [注册](https://www.rackcorp.com/signup) 一个账户。
下一个 您 可以 创建 一个 `访问 key`, 一个 `秘密 key` 和 `buckets`, 在 your
location 的 choice 与 ease. 这些 details 是 必需 用于 该 下一个 steps of
configuration, 当 `rclone config` asks 用于 您的 `access_key_id` 和 `secret_access_key`.

您的 配置 应该 end up looking 一个 bit like this:

```ini
[RCS3-demo-config]
type = s3
provider = RackCorp
env_auth = true
access_key_id = YOURACCESSKEY
secret_access_key = YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
region = au-nsw
endpoint = s3.rackcorp.com
location_constraint = au-nsw
```

### Rclone Serve S3 {#rclone}

Rclone 可以 serve 任何 远程 over 该 S3 protocol. 用于 details 参阅 the
请参见 [rclone serve s3](https://rclone.org/commands/rclone_serve_s3/) 文档。

用于 example, 到 serve `remote:path` over s3, run 该 服务器 like this:

```console
rclone serve s3 --auth-key ACCESS_KEY_ID,SECRET_ACCESS_KEY remote:path
```

这 将 是 compatible 与 一个 rclone 远程 哪个 是 defined like this:

```ini
[serves3]
type = s3
provider = Rclone
endpoint = http://127.0.0.1:8080/
access_key_id = ACCESS_KEY_ID
secret_access_key = SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
use_multipart_uploads = false
```

Note 该 设置 `use_multipart_uploads = false` 是 到 work around
[一个 bug](/commands/rclone_serve_s3/#bugs) 哪个 将 是 fixed 在 due course.

### Scaleway

[Scaleway](https://www.scaleway.com/object-storage/) 该 对象 存储 platform
allows 您 到 存储 anything 从 backups, logs 和 web assets 到 documents 和 photos.
Files 可以 是 dropped 从 该 Scaleway console 或 已传输 通过 our API and
CLI 或 使用 任何 S3-compatible tool.

Scaleway provides 一个 S3 interface 哪个 可以 是 已配置 用于 使用 与 rclone
like this:

```ini
[scaleway]
type = s3
provider = Scaleway
env_auth = false
endpoint = s3.nl-ams.scw.cloud
access_key_id = SCWXXXXXXXXXXXXXX
secret_access_key = 1111111-2222-3333-44444-55555555555555
region = nl-ams
location_constraint = nl-ams
acl = private
upload_cutoff = 5M
chunk_size = 5M
copy_cutoff = 5M
```

[Scaleway Glacier](https://www.scaleway.com/en/glacier-cold-storage/) 是
low-cost S3 Glacier alternative 从 Scaleway 和 it works 该 same way 作为 on
S3 由 accepting 该 "GLACIER" `storage_class`. 所以 您 可以 配置 您的 remote
与 该 `storage_class = GLACIER` 选项 到 上传 directly 到 Scaleway Glacier.
Don't forget 该 在 此 state 您 can't 读取 files back after, 您 将 need
到 restore them 到 "STANDARD" storage_class 第一 之前 是 able 到 read
them (参阅 "restore" section above)

### Seagate Lyve Cloud {#lyve}

[Seagate Lyve Cloud](https://www.seagate.com/gb/en/services/cloud/storage/) 是
一个 S3 compatible 对象 存储 platform 从 [Seagate](https://seagate.com/)
intended 用于 enterprise use.

这里 是 一个 配置 run 通过 用于 一个 远程 已调用 `remote` - 您 may
choose 一个 different name 的 course. Note 该 到 创建 一个 访问 key
和 秘密 密钥 您 将 need 到 创建 一个 service account first.

```console
$ rclone config
No remotes found, make a new one?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n
name> remote
```

Choose `s3` backend

```text
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
[snip]
XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
   \ (s3)
[snip]
Storage> s3
```

Choose `LyveCloud` 作为 S3 provider

```text
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
XX / Seagate Lyve Cloud
   \ (LyveCloud)
[snip]
provider> LyveCloud
```

Take 该 默认 (仅 press enter) 到 enter 访问 密钥 和 秘密 在 the
配置 file.

```text
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>
```

```text
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> XXX
```

```text
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> YYY
```

Leave 区域 blank

```text
Region to connect to.
Leave blank if you are using an S3 clone and you don't have a region.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Use this if unsure.
 1 | Will use v4 signatures and an empty region.
   \ ()
   / Use this only if v4 signatures don't work.
 2 | E.g. pre Jewel/v10 CEPH.
   \ (other-v2-signature)
region>
```

Enter 您的 Lyve Cloud endpoint. 这 字段 无法 是 kept empty.

```text
Endpoint for Lyve Cloud S3 API.
Required when using an S3 clone.
Please type in your LyveCloud endpoint.
Examples:
- s3.us-west-1.{account_name}.lyve.seagate.com (US West 1 - California)
- s3.eu-west-1.{account_name}.lyve.seagate.com (US West 1 - Ireland)
Enter a value.
endpoint> s3.us-west-1.global.lyve.seagate.com
```

Leave location constraint blank

```text
Location constraint - must be set to match the Region.
Leave blank if not sure. Used when creating buckets only.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
location_constraint>
```

Choose 默认 ACL (`private`).

```text
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
[snip]
acl>
```

和 该 配置 文件 应该 end up looking like this:

```ini
[remote]
type = s3
provider = LyveCloud
access_key_id = XXX
secret_access_key = YYY
endpoint = s3.us-east-1.lyvecloud.seagate.com
```

### SeaweedFS

[SeaweedFS](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs/) 是一个分布式存储
system 用于 blobs, objects, files, 和 data lake, 与 O(1) disk seek 和 a
scalable 文件 元数据 store. It 有 一个 S3 compatible 对象 存储 interface.
SeaweedFS 可以 也 act 作为 一个 [gateway 到 远程 S3 compatible 对象 store](https://github.com/chrislusf/seaweedfs/wiki/Gateway-to-Remote-Object-Storage)
到 cache data 和 元数据 与 asynchronous 写入 back, 用于 快速 本地 speed
和 minimize 访问 cost.

Assuming 该 SeaweedFS 是 已配置 与 `weed shell` 作为 such:

```text
> s3.bucket.create -name foo
> s3.configure -access_key=any -secret_key=any -buckets=foo -user=me -actions=Read,Write,List,Tagging,Admin -apply
{
  "identities": [
    {
      "name": "me",
      "credentials": [
        {
          "accessKey": "any",
          "secretKey": "any"
        }
      ],
      "actions": [
        "Read:foo",
        "Write:foo",
        "List:foo",
        "Tagging:foo",
        "Admin:foo"
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

到 使用 rclone 与 SeaweedFS, 以上 配置 应该 end up 与 something
like 此 在 您的 config:

```ini
[seaweedfs_s3]
type = s3
provider = SeaweedFS
access_key_id = any
secret_access_key = any
endpoint = localhost:8333
```

所以 一旦 设置 up, 用于 示例 到 复制 files 到 一个 bucket

```console
rclone copy /path/to/files seaweedfs_s3:foo
```

### Selectel

[Selectel 云存储](https://selectel.ru/services/cloud/storage/)
是 一个 S3 compatible 存储 system 哪个 features triple redundancy
storage, automatic scaling, high availability 和 一个 comprehensive IAM
system.

Selectel 有 一个 section on their website 用于 [configuring
rclone](https://docs.selectel.ru/en/cloud/object-storage/tools/rclone/)
哪个 显示 how 到 make 该 right API keys.

从 rclone v1.69 Selectel 是 一个 受支持 operator - please choose the
`Selectel` 提供者 type.

Note 该 您 应该 使用 "vHosted" 访问 用于 该 buckets (哪个 is
该 推荐 default), 不 "path style".

### Spectra Logic {#spectralogic}

[Spectra Logic](https://www.spectralogic.com/blackpearl-nearline-object-gateway)
是 一个 on-prem S3-compatible 对象 存储 gateway 该 exposes 本地 object
存储 和 policy-tiers data 到 Spectra tape 和 公共 clouds under 一个 single
namespace 用于 backup 和 archiving.

该 S3 compatible gateway 是 已配置 使用 `rclone config` 与 a
类型 的 `s3` 和 与 一个 提供者 name 的 `SpectraLogic`. 这里 是 一个 example
配置器的一个运行示例。

```text
No remotes found, make a new one?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
n/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> spectralogic

Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
[snip]
XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including ..., SpectraLogic, ...
   \ (s3)
[snip]
Storage> s3

Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
[snip]
XX / SpectraLogic BlackPearl
   \ (SpectraLogic)
[snip]
provider> SpectraLogic

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth> 1

Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> ACCESS_KEY

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> SECRET_ACCESS_KEY

Option endpoint.
Endpoint for S3 API.
Required when using an S3 clone.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
endpoint> https://bp.example.com

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n> n

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: SpectraLogic
- access_key_id: ACCESS_KEY
- secret_access_key: SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
- endpoint: https://bp.example.com
Keep this "spectratest" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

和 您的 配置 应该 end up looking like this:

```ini
[spectratest]
type = s3
provider = SpectraLogic
access_key_id = ACCESS_KEY
secret_access_key = SECRET_ACCESS_KEY
endpoint = https://bp.example.com
```

### Storj

Storj 是 一个 decentralized cloud 存储 哪个 可以 是 使用 通过 its
native protocol 或 一个 S3 compatible gateway.

该 S3 compatible gateway 是 已配置 使用 `rclone config` 与 a
类型 的 `s3` 和 与 一个 提供者 name 的 `Storj`. 这里 是 一个 example
配置器的一个运行示例。

```text
Type of storage to configure.
Storage> s3
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth> 1
Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> XXXX (as shown when creating the access grant)
Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> XXXX (as shown when creating the access grant)
Option endpoint.
Endpoint of the Shared Gateway.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / EU1 Shared Gateway
   \ (gateway.eu1.storjshare.io)
 2 / US1 Shared Gateway
   \ (gateway.us1.storjshare.io)
 3 / Asia-Pacific Shared Gateway
   \ (gateway.ap1.storjshare.io)
endpoint> 1 (as shown when creating the access grant)
Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n> n
```

Note 该 s3 凭据 是 generated 当 您 [创建 一个 access
授权](https://docs.storj.io/dcs/api-reference/s3-compatible-gateway#usage)。

#### Backend quirks

- `--chunk-size` 是 forced 到 是 64 MiB 或 greater. 这 将 使用 more
  memory 比 该 默认 的 5 MiB.
- 服务器 side 复制 是 已禁用 作为 it isn't currently 受支持 在 the
  gateway.
- GetTier 和 SetTier 是 不 supported.

#### Backend bugs

Due 到 [发出 #39](https://github.com/storj/gateway-mt/issues/39)
上传 multipart files 通过 该 S3 gateway causes them 到 lose their
metadata. 用于 rclone's purpose 此 意味着 该 该 modification time
是 不 stored, nor 是 任何 MD5SUM (如果 one 是 可用 从 the
source).

这 有 该 following consequences:

- Using `rclone rcat` 将 失败 作为 该 元数据 doesn't match 之后 upload
- Uploading files 与 `rclone mount` 将 失败 用于 该 same reason
  - 这 可以 worked around 由 使用 `--vfs-cache-mode writes` or
    `--vfs-cache-mode full` 或 设置 `--s3-upload-cutoff` large
- Files 已上传 通过 一个 multipart 上传 won't 有 their modtimes
  - 这 将 意味着 该 `rclone sync` 将 likely keep trying 到 upload
    files bigger 比 `--s3-upload-cutoff`
  - 这 可以 是 worked around 与 `--checksum` 或 `--size-only` or
    设置 `--s3-upload-cutoff` large
  - 该 maximum 值 用于 `--s3-upload-cutoff` 是 5GiB though

One 通用 purpose workaround 是 到 设置 `--s3-upload-cutoff 5G`. This
意味着 该 rclone 将 上传 files smaller 比 5GiB 作为 单个 parts.
Note 该 此 可以 是 设置 在 该 配置 文件 与 `upload_cutoff = 5G`
或 已配置 在 该 advanced settings. 如果 您 regularly transfer
files larger 比 5G 然后 使用 `--checksum` 或 `--size-only` in
`rclone sync` 是 该 推荐 workaround.

#### Comparison 与 该 native protocol

使用 该 [该 native protocol](/storj) 到 take advantage of
client-side encryption 作为 well 作为 到 achieve 该 best possible
下载 performance. Uploads 将 是 erasure-coded locally, thus a
1gb 上传 将 result 在 2.68gb 的 data 是 已上传 到 storage
nodes 跨 该 network.

使用 此 backend 和 该 S3 compatible Hosted Gateway 到 increase
上传 performance 和 reduce 该 load on 您的 systems 和 network.
Uploads 将 是 已加密 和 erasure-coded server-side, thus 一个 1GB
上传 将 result 在 仅 在 1GB 的 data 是 已上传 到 storage
nodes 跨 该 network.

用于 更多 detailed comparison please 检查 该 documentation 的 the
[storj](/storj) backend.

### Synology C2 对象 存储 {#synology-c2}

[Synology C2 对象存储](https://c2.synology.com/en-global/object-storage/overview)
provides 一个 secure, S3-compatible, 和 cost-有效 cloud 存储 solution
无 API request, 下载 fees, 和 删除 penalty.

该 S3 compatible gateway 是 已配置 使用 `rclone config` 与 a
类型 的 `s3` 和 与 一个 提供者 name 的 `Synology`. 这里 是 一个 example
配置器的一个运行示例。

首先运行：

```console
rclone config
```

这 将 guide 您 通过 一个 interactive setup process.

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config

n/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.1
name> syno

Type of storage to configure.
Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value

XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
   \ "s3"

Storage> s3

Choose your S3 provider.
Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 24 / Synology C2 Object Storage
   \ (Synology)

provider> Synology

Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default ("false").
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
   \ "false"
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
   \ "true"

env_auth> 1

AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").

access_key_id> accesskeyid

AWS Secret Access Key (password)
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").

secret_access_key> secretaccesskey

Region where your data stored.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / Europe Region 1
   \ (eu-001)
 2 / Europe Region 2
   \ (eu-002)
 3 / US Region 1
   \ (us-001)
 4 / US Region 2
   \ (us-002)
 5 / Asia (Taiwan)
   \ (tw-001)

region > 1

Option endpoint.
Endpoint for Synology C2 Object Storage API.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
 1 / EU Endpoint 1
   \ (eu-001.s3.synologyc2.net)
 2 / US Endpoint 1
   \ (us-001.s3.synologyc2.net)
 3 / TW Endpoint 1
   \ (tw-001.s3.synologyc2.net)

endpoint> 1

Option location_constraint.
Location constraint - must be set to match the Region.
Leave blank if not sure. Used when creating buckets only.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
location_constraint>

Edit advanced config? (y/n)
y) Yes
n) No
y/n> y

Option no_check_bucket.
If set, don't attempt to check the bucket exists or create it.
This can be useful when trying to minimise the number of transactions
rclone does if you know the bucket exists already.
It can also be needed if the user you are using does not have bucket
creation permissions. Before v1.52.0 this would have passed silently
due to a bug.
Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default (true).

no_check_bucket> true

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: Synology
- region: eu-001
- endpoint: eu-001.s3.synologyc2.net
- no_check_bucket: true
Keep this "syno" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote

y/e/d> y
```

### Tencent COS {#tencent-cos}

[Tencent Cloud 对象 存储 (COS)](https://intl.cloud.tencent.com/product/cos)
是 一个 distributed 存储 service offered 由 Tencent Cloud 用于 unstructured data.
It 是 secure, stable, massive, convenient, low-delay 和 low-cost.

到 配置 访问 到 Tencent COS, follow 该 steps below:

1. Run `rclone config` 和 select `n` 用于 一个 新 remote.

   ```text
   rclone config
   No remotes found, make a new one?
   n) New remote
   s) Set configuration password
   q) Quit config
   n/s/q> n
   ```

2. Give 该 name 的 该 configuration. 用于 example, name it 'cos'.

   ```text
   name> cos
   ```

3. Select `s3` storage.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   [snip]
   XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
      \ "s3"
   [snip]
   Storage> s3
   ```

4. Select `TencentCOS` provider.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   1 / Amazon Web Services (AWS) S3
      \ "AWS"
   [snip]
   11 / Tencent Cloud Object Storage (COS)
      \ "TencentCOS"
   [snip]
   provider> TencentCOS
   ```

5. Enter 您的 SecretId 和 SecretKey 的 Tencent Cloud.

   ```text
   Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
   Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
   Enter a boolean value (true or false). Press Enter for the default ("false").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
      \ "false"
    2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
      \ "true"
   env_auth> 1
   AWS Access Key ID.
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   access_key_id> AKIDxxxxxxxxxx
   AWS Secret Access Key (password)
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   secret_access_key> xxxxxxxxxxx
   ```

6. Select 端点 用于 Tencent COS. 这 是 该 standard 端点 用于 different region.

   ```text
    1 / Beijing Region.
      \ "cos.ap-beijing.myqcloud.com"
    2 / Nanjing Region.
      \ "cos.ap-nanjing.myqcloud.com"
    3 / Shanghai Region.
      \ "cos.ap-shanghai.myqcloud.com"
    4 / Guangzhou Region.
      \ "cos.ap-guangzhou.myqcloud.com"
   [snip]
   endpoint> 4
   ```

7. Choose acl 和 存储 class.

   ```text
   Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
   doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Owner gets Full_CONTROL. No one else has access rights (default).
      \ "default"
   [snip]
   acl> 1
   The storage class to use when storing new objects in Tencent COS.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Default
      \ ""
   [snip]
   storage_class> 1
   Edit advanced config? (y/n)
   y) Yes
   n) No (default)
   y/n> n
   Remote config
   --------------------
   [cos]
   type = s3
   provider = TencentCOS
   env_auth = false
   access_key_id = xxx
   secret_access_key = xxx
   endpoint = cos.ap-guangzhou.myqcloud.com
   acl = default
   --------------------
   y) Yes this is OK (default)
   e) Edit this remote
   d) Delete this remote
   y/e/d> y
   Current remotes:

   Name                 Type
   ====                 ====
   cos                  s3
   ```

#### Tencent COS Global Acceleration Endpoint

当 使用 该 Global Acceleration 端点 (`cos.accelerate.myqcloud.com`),
rclone automatically 设置 `no_check_bucket = true` 因为 此 acceleration
端点 确实 不 支持 该 `CreateBucket` 调用 哪个 是 使用 用于 ensuring
一个 bucket's existence 由 rclone. Global Acceleration 是 一个 per-桶 feature,
所以 您 应该 第一 创建 该 桶 在 one physical region, 然后 启用 it
在 该 Tencent Cloud console.

### US3 {#us3}
[US3](https://www.ucloud.cn/site/product/ufile.html) 对象 存储 是 一个 service 该 provides cloud 存储 用于 unstructured files 用于 internet applications.

到 配置 访问 到 US3, follow 该 steps below:
1. 第一 run:
    ```console
    rclone config
    No remotes found, make a new one?
    n) New remote
    s) Set configuration password
    q) Quit config
    n/s/q> n
    ```
2. Give 该 name 的 该 configuration. 用于 example, name it 'US3'.

   ```text
   name> US3
   ```
3. Select `s3` storage.

   ```text
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   [snip]
   XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
      \ "s3"
   [snip]
   Storage> s3
   ```
4. Select `US3` provider.

   ```text
    Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
    XX / Amazon Web Services (AWS) S3
       \ (AWS)
    [snip]
    XX / UCloud Object Storage (US3)
       \ (US3)
    [snip]
    provider> US3
   ```
5. Enter 您的 SecretId 和 SecretKey 的 US3.

   ```text
   Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
   Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
   Press Enter for the default (false).
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
      \ "false"
    2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
      \ "true"
   env_auth> 1
   Option access_key_id.
   AWS Access Key ID.
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
   access_key_id> AKIDxxxxxxxxxx
   AWS Secret Access Key (password)
   Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   secret_access_key> xxxxxxxxxxx
   ```

6. Select endpoint.
   ```text
    Option endpoint.
    Endpoint for S3 API.
    Required when using an S3 clone.
    Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
    Press Enter to leave empty.
    1 / North China (Beijing 2).
      \ "s3-cn-bj.ufileos.com"
    2 / North China (Ulanqab).
      \ "s3-cn-wlcb.ufileos.com"
    3 / Shanghai.
      \ "s3-cn-sh2.ufileos.com"
    4 / South China (Guangzhou).
      \ "s3-cn-gd.ufileos.com"
   [snip]
   endpoint> 1
   ```

7. Choose acl 和 存储 class.

   ```text
   Option acl.
   Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
   This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
   For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
   Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
   doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
   If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
   the default (private) will be used.
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
   Press Enter to leave empty.
     / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
   1 | No one else has access rights (default).
     \ (private)
     / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
   2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
     \ (public-read)
   acl> 1

   The storage class to use when storing new objects in US3.
   Enter a string value. Press Enter for the default ("").
   Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
    1 / Default
      \ ""
   [snip]
   storage_class> 1
   Edit advanced config? (y/n)
   y) Yes
   n) No (default)
   y/n> n

    Configuration complete.
    Options:
    - type: s3
    - provider: US3
    - access_key_id: xx
    - secret_access_key: xx
    - endpoint: s3-cn-bj.ufileos.com
    - acl: private

    Keep this "US3" remote?
    y) Yes this is OK (default)
    e) Edit this remote
    d) Delete this remote
    y/e/d> y
    Current remotes:

    Name                 Type
    ====                 ====
    US3                  s3
    ```

### Wasabi

[Wasabi](https://wasabi.com) 是一项基于云的对象存储服务，适用于各种
广泛的应用和使用场景。Wasabi 专为需要高性能、

可靠且安全的数据存储基础设施的个人和组织而设计，且成本极低。

Wasabi 提供了一个 S3 接口，可以按如下方式配置以供
rclone 使用。

```text
No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
n/s> n
name> wasabi
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
[snip]
XX / Amazon S3 (also Dreamhost, Ceph, ChinaMobile, ArvanCloud, Minio, Liara)
   \ "s3"
[snip]
Storage> s3
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars). Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step
   \ "false"
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM)
   \ "true"
env_auth> 1
AWS Access Key ID - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
access_key_id> YOURACCESSKEY
AWS Secret Access Key (password) - leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
secret_access_key> YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
Region to connect to.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
   / The default endpoint - a good choice if you are unsure.
 1 | US Region, Northern Virginia, or Pacific Northwest.
   | Leave location constraint empty.
   \ "us-east-1"
[snip]
region> us-east-1
Endpoint for S3 API.
Leave blank if using AWS to use the default endpoint for the region.
Specify if using an S3 clone such as Ceph.
endpoint> s3.wasabisys.com
Location constraint - must be set to match the Region. Used when creating buckets only.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Empty for US Region, Northern Virginia, or Pacific Northwest.
   \ ""
[snip]
location_constraint>
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and/or storing objects in S3.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL. No one else has access rights (default).
   \ "private"
[snip]
acl>
The server-side encryption algorithm used when storing this object in S3.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / None
   \ ""
 2 / AES256
   \ "AES256"
server_side_encryption>
The storage class to use when storing objects in S3.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value
 1 / Default
   \ ""
 2 / Standard storage class
   \ "STANDARD"
 3 / Reduced redundancy storage class
   \ "REDUCED_REDUNDANCY"
 4 / Standard Infrequent Access storage class
   \ "STANDARD_IA"
storage_class>
Remote config
--------------------
[wasabi]
env_auth = false
access_key_id = YOURACCESSKEY
secret_access_key = YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
region = us-east-1
endpoint = s3.wasabisys.com
location_constraint =
acl =
server_side_encryption =
storage_class =
--------------------
y) Yes this is OK
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

这将使配置文件看起来如下所示。

```ini
[wasabi]
type = s3
provider = Wasabi
env_auth = false
access_key_id = YOURACCESSKEY
secret_access_key = YOURSECRETACCESSKEY
region =
endpoint = s3.wasabisys.com
location_constraint =
acl =
server_side_encryption =
storage_class =
```

### Zadara 对象存储 {#zadara}

[Zadara 对象存储](https://www.zadara.com) 是一个完全托管的、
企业级 S3 兼容存储解决方案，提供可扩展的、
多租户对象存储，具有灵活的部署选项（本地、
混合或云）。

可以使用 `rclone config` 配置 Zadara 对象存储，其中 `s3` 作为
存储类型，`Zadara` 作为提供者名称。以下是
配置器的一个运行示例。

认证和端点信息（包括 区域 字段）应从 Zadara 的对象存储
管理界面获取。

要配置对 Zadara 对象存储的访问，请先运行：

```console
rclone config
```

```text
This will guide you through an interactive setup process:

No remotes found, make a new one\?
n) New remote
s) Set configuration password
n/s> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> Zadara-Object-Storage

Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.

 XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS ...
   \ (s3)

Storage> s3

Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.

XX / Zadara Object Storage
   \ (Zadara)

provider> Zadara

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>

Option access_key_id.
AWS Access Key ID.
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
access_key_id> S3_ACCESS_KEY

Option secret_access_key.
AWS Secret Access Key (password).
Leave blank for anonymous access or runtime credentials.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
secret_access_key> S3_SECRET_KEY

Option region.
Region to connect to.
Leave blank if you are using an S3 clone and you don't have a region.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / The default region.
 1 | Leave location constraint empty.
   \ (us-east-1)
region>

Option endpoint.
Endpoint for S3 API.
Required when using an S3 clone.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
endpoint> https://vsa-00000001-public-zadara-cloud-01.zadarazios.com

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n>

Configuration complete.
Options:
- type: s3
- provider: Zadara
- access_key_id: S3_ACCESS_KEY
- secret_access_key: S3_SECRET_KEY
- endpoint: https://vsa-00000001-public-zadara-cloud-01.zadarazios.com
Keep this "Zadara-Object-Storage" remote?
y) Yes this is OK (default)
e) Edit this remote
d) Delete this remote
y/e/d> y
```

这将使配置文件看起来如下所示。

```ini
[Zadara-Object-Storage]
type = s3
provider = Zadara
access_key_id = S3_ACCESS_KEY
secret_access_key = S3_SECRET_KEY
endpoint = https://vsa-00000001-public-zadara-cloud-01.zadarazios.com
```

### Zata 对象存储 {#Zata}

[Zata 对象存储](https://zata.ai/) 提供安全、S3 兼容的云
存储解决方案，专为可扩展性和性能而设计，适用于各种
数据存储需求。

首先运行：

```console
rclone config
```

```text

e) Edit existing remote
n) New remote
d) Delete remote
r) Rename remote
c) Copy remote
s) Set configuration password
q) Quit config
e/n/d/r/c/s/q> n

Enter name for new remote.
name> my zata storage

Option Storage.
Type of storage to configure.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.

XX / Amazon S3 Compliant Storage Providers including AWS, ...
   \ (s3)

Storage> s3

Option provider.
Choose your S3 provider.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.

XX / Zata (S3 compatible Gateway)
   \ (Zata)

Option env_auth.
Get AWS credentials from runtime (environment variables or EC2/ECS meta data if no env vars).
Only applies if access_key_id and secret_access_key is blank.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own boolean value (true or false).
Press Enter for the default (false).
 1 / Enter AWS credentials in the next step.
   \ (false)
 2 / Get AWS credentials from the environment (env vars or IAM).
   \ (true)
env_auth>

   \ (us-east-1)

   \ (idr01.zata.ai)

Option location_constraint.
Location constraint - must be set to match the Region.
Leave blank if not sure. Used when creating buckets only.
Enter a value. Press Enter to leave empty.
location_constraint>

Option acl.
Canned ACL used when creating buckets and storing or copying objects.
This ACL is used for creating objects and if bucket_acl isn't set, for creating buckets too.
For more info visit https://docs.aws.amazon.com/AmazonS3/latest/dev/acl-overview.html#canned-acl
Note that this ACL is applied when server-side copying objects as S3
doesn't copy the ACL from the source but rather writes a fresh one.
If the acl is an empty string then no X-Amz-Acl: header is added and
the default (private) will be used.
Choose a number from below, or type in your own value.
Press Enter to leave empty.
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 1 | No one else has access rights (default).
   \ (private)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 2 | The AllUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (public-read)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 3 | The AllUsers group gets READ and WRITE access.
   | Granting this on a bucket is generally not recommended.
   \ (public-read-write)
   / Owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 4 | The AuthenticatedUsers group gets READ access.
   \ (authenticated-read)
   / Object owner gets FULL_CONTROL.
 5 | Bucket owner gets READ access.
   | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-read)
   / Both the object owner and the bucket owner get FULL_CONTROL over the object.
 6 | If you specify this canned ACL when creating a bucket, Amazon S3 ignores it.
   \ (bucket-owner-full-control)
acl>

Edit advanced config?
y) Yes
n) No (default)
y/n>
```

## 内存使用 {#memory}

rclone 占用大量内存的最常见原因是单个目录中
包含数百万个文件。尽管 s3 实际上并没有
目录的概念，但为了与普通文件系统兼容，rclone
按目录逐个进行同步。

rclone 将每个目录作为 rclone 对象加载到内存中。每个 rclone
对象占用 0.5k-1k 内存，因此每 1,000,000 个文件
约需 1GB 内存，并且该目录的同步在该目录完全
加载到内存后才会开始。因此对于大型目录，同步
可能需要很长时间才能启动。

要同步包含 100,000,000 个文件的目录，您需要大约
100 GB 内存。在某个时刻，内存量变得难以提供，
因此有一个
[一个解决方法](https://github.com/rclone/rclone/wiki/Big-syncs-with-millions-of-files)
涉及少量脚本编写。

在某个时刻，rclone 将获得一种同步模式，实际上就是
内置到 rclone 中的此变通方法。

## 限制

`rclone about` 不受 S3 后端支持。没有此功能的后端
无法确定 rclone 挂载的可用空间，也不能在
rclone union 远程成员中使用 `mfs`（最多可用空间）
策略。

请参阅[不支持 rclone 关于 的后端列表](https://rclone.org/overview/#optional-features)
和 [rclone about](https://rclone.org/commands/rclone_about/)。
